text: "156\nHOUR OF PRAYER. 8, 8, 8, 4, or 8, 8, 8, 6. (New.)\n1. My God! is\n-b-4-2\nb\n9-b-b\n26-b\nan\n-\nTHE CHURCH:\ny\nhour so sweet From blush of morn to\nAs that which calls me to\nthy feet-The hour\n431\nThe hour of prayer.\n2 Blest is the tranquil hour of morn,\nAnd blest that hour of solemn eve,\nWhen, on the wings of prayer up-borne,\nThe world I leave.\n3 Then is my strength by thee renewed;\nThen are my sins by thee forgiven;\nThen dost thou cheer my solitude\nWith hopes of heaven.\n4 No words can tell what sweet relief\nThere for my every want I find;\nWhat strength for warfare, balm for grief,\nWhat peace of mind!\nCop\n(581) | 3 When mystery clouds my darkened path,\nI\'ll check my dread, my doubts reprove;\nIn this my soul sweet comfort hath,\nThat God is love!\n5 Hushed is each doubt, gone every fear;\nMy spirit seems in heaven to stay;\nAnd e\'en the penitential tear\nIs wiped away.\n432\nGod is love.\n1 I can not always trace the way\nWhere thou, almighty One, dost move;\nBut I can always, always say,\nThat God is love.\n(86)\n2 When fear her chilling mantle flings\nO\'er earth, my soul to heaven above,\nAs to her native home, upsprings;\nFor God is love.\nJ. P. POWELL.\nevening star,\nof prayer.\n4 Oh may this truth my heart employ,\nAnd every gloomy thought remove;\nIt fills my soul with boundless joy,\nThat God is love!\n433\nThy will be done.\n(900)\n1 My God, my Father, while I stray\nOh, teach me from my heart to say,\nFar from my home, on life\'s rough way,\n\"Thy will be done!\"\n2 What though in lonely grief I sigh\nFor friends beloved no longer nigh;\nSubmissive still would I reply,\n\"Thy will be done!\nOriel, Key Ab. Delaware, Key Ab.\n3 If thou shouldst call me to resign\nWhat most I prize-it ne\'er was mine,\nI only yield thee what was thine:\n\"Thy will be done!\"\n4 If but my fainting heart be blest\nWith thy sweet Spirit for its guest,\nMy God, to thee I leave the rest:\n\"Thy will be done!\""
